## å…ƒèµ„æº

* [Wikipedia Text-to-video model](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Text-to-video_model)

  * > A **text-to-video model** is a [machine learning](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Machine_learning) model which takes as input a [natural language](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Natural_language) description and produces a [video](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Video) matching that description.[[1\]](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Text-to-video_model#cite_note-AIIR-1)
    > æ–‡æœ¬åˆ°è§†é¢‘æ¨¡åž‹æ˜¯ä¸€ç§æœºå™¨å­¦ä¹ æ¨¡åž‹ï¼Œå®ƒå°†è‡ªç„¶è¯­è¨€æè¿°ä½œä¸ºè¾“å…¥å¹¶ç”Ÿæˆä¸Žè¯¥æè¿°åŒ¹é…çš„è§†é¢‘ã€‚ [[1\]](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Text-to-video_model#cite_note-AIIR-1)
  >
    > Video prediction on making objects realistic in a stable background is performed by using [recurrent neural network](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Recurrent_neural_network) for a sequence to sequence model with a connector [convolutional neural network](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Convolutional_neural_network) encoding and decoding each frame pixel by pixel,[[2\]](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Text-to-video_model#cite_note-2) creating video using [deep learning](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Deep_learning).[[3\]](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Text-to-video_model#cite_note-3)
    > é€šè¿‡ä½¿ç”¨å¾ªçŽ¯ç¥žç»ç½‘ç»œè¿›è¡Œåºåˆ—åˆ°åºåˆ—æ¨¡åž‹çš„è§†é¢‘é¢„æµ‹ï¼Œä½¿å¯¹è±¡åœ¨ç¨³å®šçš„èƒŒæ™¯ä¸‹å…·æœ‰è¿žæŽ¥å™¨å·ç§¯ç¥žç»ç½‘ç»œé€åƒç´ ç¼–ç å’Œè§£ç æ¯ä¸ªå¸§ï¼Œ [[2\]](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Text-to-video_model#cite_note-2) ä½¿ç”¨æ·±åº¦å­¦ä¹ åˆ›å»ºè§†é¢‘ã€‚ [[3\]](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Text-to-video_model#cite_note-3)

Gen-2 Explainedï¼ˆGen-2 è§£é‡Šï¼‰ï¼š

> Not too long ago, runway pushed the boundaries of generative Ai with Gen One a video to video model that allows you to use words and images to generate new videos out of existing ones in the week since launching, the model has constantly gotten better temporal consistency, better fidelity better results and as more and more people gained access, we unlocked entirely new use cases and displays of creativity and today we're excited to announce our biggest unlock yettext to Video with Gen Two now. You can generate a video with nothing but words, no driving video no input image gen 2 represents yet another major research milestone and another monumental step forward for generative Ai with Gen 2, anyone anywhere can suddenly realize entire worlds, animations stories anything you can imagine gen two coming, very soon to https://runwayml.com/
>

äººå·¥æ™ºèƒ½ã€è§†é¢‘ç”Ÿæˆã€ç”Ÿæˆå¼äººå·¥æ™ºèƒ½ã€Runway



Gen-1 Explainedï¼ˆGen-1 è§£é‡Šï¼‰ï¼š

> Gen 1 is able to realistically and consistently apply the composition and style of an image or text prompt to the target video allowing you to generate new video content using an existing video.We call this approach video to video, and we're incredibly excited to share a few early use casesstylization mode, transfer the style of any image or prompt to every frame of your video storyboard mode, turn mockups into fully stylized and animated rendersmask mode, isolate subjects in your video and modify them with simple text prompts.Render mode, turn untextured renders into realistic outputs by applying an input imageor prompt.
> To realizing the future of storytelling.
>
> Gen 1 èƒ½å¤Ÿé€¼çœŸä¸”ä¸€è‡´åœ°å°†å›¾åƒæˆ–æ–‡æœ¬æç¤ºçš„æž„å›¾å’Œæ ·å¼åº”ç”¨äºŽç›®æ ‡è§†é¢‘ï¼Œä»Žè€Œå…è®¸æ‚¨ä½¿ç”¨çŽ°æœ‰è§†é¢‘ç”Ÿæˆæ–°çš„è§†é¢‘å†…å®¹ã€‚æˆ‘ä»¬å°†è¿™ç§æ–¹æ³•ç§°ä¸ºè§†é¢‘åˆ°è§†é¢‘ï¼Œæˆ‘ä»¬éžå¸¸é«˜å…´åœ°åˆ†äº«ä¸€äº›æ—©æœŸçš„ç”¨ä¾‹é£Žæ ¼åŒ–æ¨¡å¼ï¼Œå°†ä»»ä½•å›¾åƒæˆ–æç¤ºçš„æ ·å¼ä¼ è¾“åˆ°è§†é¢‘æ•…äº‹æ¿æ¨¡å¼çš„æ¯ä¸€å¸§ï¼Œå°†æ¨¡åž‹è½¬æ¢ä¸ºå®Œå…¨é£Žæ ¼åŒ–å’ŒåŠ¨ç”»æ¸²æŸ“è’™ç‰ˆæ¨¡å¼ï¼Œéš”ç¦»è§†é¢‘ä¸­çš„ä¸»é¢˜å¹¶ä½¿ç”¨ç®€å•çš„æ–‡æœ¬æç¤ºå¯¹å…¶è¿›è¡Œä¿®æ”¹ã€‚æ¸²æŸ“æ¨¡å¼ï¼Œé€šè¿‡åº”ç”¨è¾“å…¥å›¾åƒæˆ–æç¤ºå°†æ— çº¹ç†æ¸²æŸ“è½¬æ¢ä¸ºé€¼çœŸçš„è¾“å‡ºã€‚

### 7ã€å¾®è½¯çš„GAIA

Introducing ï¼ˆä»‹ç»ï¼‰: GAIA, which stands for Generative AI for Avatar, is a project that focuses on zero-shot talking avatar generation, It aims at synthesizing natural talking videos from speech and a single portrait image. 

GAIAä»£è¡¨Generative AI for Avatarï¼Œæ˜¯ä¸€ä¸ªä¸“æ³¨äºŽé›¶é•œå¤´è¯´è¯å¤´åƒç”Ÿæˆçš„é¡¹ç›®ã€‚å®ƒæ—¨åœ¨ä»Žè¯­éŸ³å’Œå•ä¸ªè‚–åƒå›¾åƒä¸­åˆæˆè‡ªç„¶çš„è¯´è¯è§†é¢‘ã€‚



Websiteï¼ˆå®˜æ–¹ç½‘ç«™ï¼‰: https://microsoft.github.io/GAIA/       12æœˆ14æ—¥ã€28æ—¥è®¿é—®è¯¥ç½‘é¡µæ˜¾ç¤º404é”™è¯¯

### 8ã€GitHub - arpitbansal297/Universal-Guided-Diffusion

Introducing ï¼ˆä»‹ç»ï¼‰:  A GitHub repository for Universal Guided Diffusion.

ä¸€ä¸ªé€šç”¨å¼•å¯¼æ‰©æ•£çš„ GitHub å­˜å‚¨åº“ã€‚



Paperï¼ˆè®ºæ–‡åœ°å€ï¼‰: 2023 [Universal Guidance for Diffusion Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2302.07121v1)

GitHubï¼ˆä»£ç åœ°å€ï¼‰ï¼šhttps://github.com/arpitbansal297/Universal-Guided-Diffusion

Newsletter Post Titleï¼ˆæ—¶äº‹é€šè®¯å¸–å­æ ‡é¢˜ï¼‰ï¼šAI in the workplace

Newsletter Post URLï¼ˆæ—¶äº‹é€šè®¯å¸–å­ç½‘å€ï¼‰ï¼š

* [AI in the workplace](https://bensbites.beehiiv.com/p/ai-workplace)
  * > Multimodal universal guidance for diffusion models without retraining.

Dateï¼ˆæ—¥æœŸï¼‰ï¼š2023å¹´6æœˆ8æ—¥



Summaryï¼ˆæ€»ç»“ï¼‰ï¼š

> This is a GitHub repository for Universal Guided Diffusion, which is a machine learning model for image and video generation. 
>
> è¿™æ˜¯é€šç”¨å¼•å¯¼æ‰©æ•£çš„ GitHub å­˜å‚¨åº“ï¼Œé€šç”¨å¼•å¯¼æ‰©æ•£æ˜¯ä¸€ç§ç”¨äºŽå›¾åƒå’Œè§†é¢‘ç”Ÿæˆçš„æœºå™¨å­¦ä¹ æ¨¡åž‹ã€‚
>



Tagsï¼ˆæ ‡ç­¾ï¼‰ï¼š

machine learning, image generation, video generation, GitHub

æœºå™¨å­¦ä¹ ã€å›¾åƒç”Ÿæˆã€è§†é¢‘ç”Ÿæˆã€GitHub



Media information åª’ä½“èµ„è®¯ï¼š

* [Universal-Guided-Diffusion/README.md at main Â· arpitbansal297/Universal-Guided-Diffusion](https://github.com/arpitbansal297/Universal-Guided-Diffusion/blob/main/README.md)
  * > The official PyTorch implementation of [Universal Guidance for Diffusion Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2302.07121). This repository has python implementation of universal guidance algorithm that enables controlling diffusion models by arbitrary guidance modalities without the need to retrain any use-specific components. Different guidance modalities we demonstrate are Human Identity, Segmentation Maps, Object Location, Image Style and Clip. Our implementation is based on the text-to-img model from [Stable Diffusion](https://github.com/CompVis/stable-diffusion) and Imagenet Diffusion Model from [OpenAI's guided diffusion](https://github.com/openai/guided-diffusion).
    > æ‰©æ•£æ¨¡åž‹é€šç”¨æŒ‡å—çš„å®˜æ–¹ PyTorch å®žçŽ°ã€‚è¯¥å­˜å‚¨åº“å…·æœ‰é€šç”¨åˆ¶å¯¼ç®—æ³•çš„ python å®žçŽ°ï¼Œå¯ä»¥é€šè¿‡ä»»æ„åˆ¶å¯¼æ–¹å¼æŽ§åˆ¶æ‰©æ•£æ¨¡åž‹ï¼Œè€Œæ— éœ€é‡æ–°è®­ç»ƒä»»ä½•ç‰¹å®šç”¨é€”çš„ç»„ä»¶ã€‚æˆ‘ä»¬å±•ç¤ºçš„ä¸åŒå¼•å¯¼æ¨¡å¼åŒ…æ‹¬äººç±»èº«ä»½ã€åˆ†å‰²å›¾ã€å¯¹è±¡ä½ç½®ã€å›¾åƒæ ·å¼å’Œå‰ªè¾‘ã€‚æˆ‘ä»¬çš„å®žçŽ°åŸºäºŽæ¥è‡ªç¨³å®šæ‰©æ•£çš„æ–‡æœ¬åˆ°å›¾åƒæ¨¡åž‹å’Œæ¥è‡ª OpenAI å¼•å¯¼æ‰©æ•£çš„ Imagenet æ‰©æ•£æ¨¡åž‹ã€‚

* [Universal Guidance for Diffusion Models,arXiv - CS - Machine Learning - X-MOL](https://newsletter.x-mol.com/paper/1626022089827893248?adv)

  * > **æ‰©æ•£æ¨¡åž‹çš„é€šç”¨æŒ‡å—**

    >
      > å…¸åž‹çš„æ‰©æ•£æ¨¡åž‹ç»è¿‡è®­ç»ƒå¯ä»¥æŽ¥å—ç‰¹å®šå½¢å¼çš„è°ƒèŠ‚ï¼Œæœ€å¸¸è§çš„æ˜¯æ–‡æœ¬ï¼Œå¹¶ä¸”ä¸èƒ½åœ¨æ²¡æœ‰é‡æ–°è®­ç»ƒçš„æƒ…å†µä¸‹ä»¥å…¶ä»–å½¢å¼ä¸ºæ¡ä»¶ã€‚åœ¨è¿™é¡¹å·¥ä½œä¸­ï¼Œæˆ‘ä»¬æå‡ºäº†ä¸€ç§é€šç”¨çš„æŒ‡å¯¼ç®—æ³•ï¼Œä½¿æ‰©æ•£æ¨¡åž‹èƒ½å¤Ÿç”±ä»»æ„æŒ‡å¯¼æ–¹å¼æŽ§åˆ¶ï¼Œè€Œæ— éœ€é‡æ–°è®­ç»ƒä»»ä½•ç‰¹å®šäºŽä½¿ç”¨çš„ç»„ä»¶ã€‚æˆ‘ä»¬å±•ç¤ºäº†æˆ‘ä»¬çš„ç®—æ³•æˆåŠŸåœ°ç”Ÿæˆäº†å…·æœ‰å¼•å¯¼åŠŸèƒ½çš„é«˜è´¨é‡å›¾åƒï¼ŒåŒ…æ‹¬åˆ†å‰²ã€äººè„¸è¯†åˆ«ã€å¯¹è±¡æ£€æµ‹å’Œåˆ†ç±»å™¨ä¿¡å·ã€‚ä»£ç å¯åœ¨ https://github.com/arpitbansal297/Universal-Guided-Diffusion èŽ·å¾—ã€‚

### 9ã€SceneScape: Text-Driven Consistent Scene Generation

Introducing ï¼ˆä»‹ç»ï¼‰: A method for text-driven perpetual view generation, which synthesizes long-term videos of various scenes solely based on an input text prompt.

ä¸€ç§æ–‡æœ¬é©±åŠ¨çš„æ°¸ä¹…è§†å›¾ç”Ÿæˆæ–¹æ³•ï¼Œè¯¥æ–¹æ³•ä»…æ ¹æ®è¾“å…¥çš„æ–‡æœ¬æç¤ºåˆæˆå„ç§åœºæ™¯çš„é•¿æœŸè§†é¢‘ã€‚



Websiteï¼ˆå®˜æ–¹ç½‘ç«™ï¼‰: https://scenescape.github.io/

Paperï¼ˆè®ºæ–‡åœ°å€ï¼‰: 2023 [SceneScape: Text-Driven Consistent Scene Generation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2302.01133)

Supplementary Materialï¼ˆè¡¥å……ææ–™ç½‘å€ï¼‰ï¼šhttps://scenescape.github.io/sm/index.html

GitHubï¼ˆä»£ç åœ°å€ï¼‰ï¼šhttps://github.com/RafailFridman/SceneScape

Dateï¼ˆæ—¥æœŸï¼‰ï¼š2023å¹´2æœˆ3æ—¥



Summaryï¼ˆæ€»ç»“ï¼‰ï¼š

> The paper presents a method for text-driven perpetual view generation, which synthesizes long-term videos of various scenes solely based on an input text prompt. The method combines the generative power of a pre-trained text-to-image model with the geometric priors learned by a pre-trained monocular depth prediction model to achieve 3D consistency. The depth maps are used to construct a unified mesh representation of the scene, which is progressively constructed along the video generation process. The method generates diverse scenes, such as walkthroughs in spaceships, caves, or ice castles. 
>
> æœ¬æ–‡æå‡ºäº†ä¸€ç§æ–‡æœ¬é©±åŠ¨çš„æ°¸ä¹…è§†å›¾ç”Ÿæˆæ–¹æ³•ï¼Œè¯¥æ–¹æ³•ä»…æ ¹æ®è¾“å…¥çš„æ–‡æœ¬æç¤ºåˆæˆå„ç§åœºæ™¯çš„é•¿æœŸè§†é¢‘ã€‚è¯¥æ–¹æ³•å°†é¢„è®­ç»ƒçš„æ–‡æœ¬åˆ°å›¾åƒæ¨¡åž‹çš„ç”Ÿæˆèƒ½åŠ›ä¸Žé¢„è®­ç»ƒçš„å•ç›®æ·±åº¦é¢„æµ‹æ¨¡åž‹å­¦ä¹ çš„å‡ ä½•å…ˆéªŒç›¸ç»“åˆï¼Œä»¥å®žçŽ° 3D ä¸€è‡´æ€§ã€‚æ·±åº¦å›¾ç”¨äºŽæž„å»ºåœºæ™¯çš„ç»Ÿä¸€ç½‘æ ¼è¡¨ç¤ºï¼Œè¯¥è¡¨ç¤ºæ˜¯æ²¿ç€è§†é¢‘ç”Ÿæˆè¿‡ç¨‹é€æ­¥æž„å»ºçš„ã€‚è¯¥æ–¹æ³•ç”Ÿæˆä¸åŒçš„åœºæ™¯ï¼Œä¾‹å¦‚å®‡å®™é£žèˆ¹ã€æ´žç©´æˆ–å†°å ¡ä¸­çš„æ¼”ç»ƒã€‚
>
> How It Worksï¼ˆå·¥ä½œåŽŸç†ï¼‰ ï¼š
>
> > ```
> > We represent the generated scene with a unified mesh îˆ¹, which is constructed in an online fashion. Given a camera at Ct+1, at each synthesis step, a new frame is generated by projecting îˆ¹t into Ct+1, and synthesizing the newly revealed content by using a pre-trained text-to-image diffusion model. To estimate the geometry of the new synthesized content, we leverage a pre-trained depth prediction model; to ensure the predicted depth is consistent with the existing scene îˆ¹t, we deploy a test-time training, encouraging the predicted depth by the model to match the projected depth from îˆ¹t. We then update our mesh representation to form îˆ¹t+1 which includes the new scene content.
> >  
> > æˆ‘ä»¬ç”¨ç»Ÿä¸€çš„ç½‘æ ¼ îˆ¹ è¡¨ç¤ºç”Ÿæˆçš„åœºæ™¯ï¼Œè¯¥ç½‘æ ¼ä»¥åœ¨çº¿æ–¹å¼æž„å»ºã€‚ç»™å®š Ct+1 å¤„çš„ç›¸æœºï¼Œåœ¨æ¯ä¸ªåˆæˆæ­¥éª¤ä¸­ï¼Œé€šè¿‡å°† îˆ¹t æŠ•å½±åˆ° Ct+1 ä¸­ç”Ÿæˆä¸€ä¸ªæ–°å¸§ï¼Œå¹¶ä½¿ç”¨ pre åˆæˆæ–°æ˜¾ç¤ºçš„å†…å®¹-è®­ç»ƒæœ‰ç´ çš„æ–‡æœ¬åˆ°å›¾åƒæ‰©æ•£æ¨¡åž‹ã€‚ä¸ºäº†ä¼°è®¡æ–°åˆæˆå†…å®¹çš„å‡ ä½•å½¢çŠ¶ï¼Œæˆ‘ä»¬åˆ©ç”¨é¢„å…ˆè®­ç»ƒçš„æ·±åº¦é¢„æµ‹æ¨¡åž‹ï¼›ä¸ºäº†ç¡®ä¿é¢„æµ‹æ·±åº¦ä¸ŽçŽ°æœ‰åœºæ™¯ îˆ¹t ä¸€è‡´ï¼Œæˆ‘ä»¬éƒ¨ç½²äº†æµ‹è¯•æ—¶è®­ç»ƒï¼Œé¼“åŠ±æ¨¡åž‹çš„é¢„æµ‹æ·±åº¦ä¸Ž îˆ¹t çš„é¢„æµ‹æ·±åº¦ç›¸åŒ¹é…ã€‚ç„¶åŽï¼Œæˆ‘ä»¬æ›´æ–°ç½‘æ ¼è¡¨ç¤ºä»¥å½¢æˆ îˆ¹t+1 ï¼Œå…¶ä¸­åŒ…æ‹¬æ–°çš„åœºæ™¯å†…å®¹ã€‚
> >  
> >  
> >  A visualization of the resulting meshes, produced by our method and post processed with Poisson surface reconstruction.
> > ç»“æžœç½‘æ ¼çš„å¯è§†åŒ–ï¼Œç”±æˆ‘ä»¬çš„æ–¹æ³•ç”Ÿæˆå¹¶é€šè¿‡æ³Šæ¾æ›²é¢é‡å»ºè¿›è¡ŒåŽå¤„ç†ã€‚
> > ```
>



Tagsï¼ˆæ ‡ç­¾ï¼‰ï¼š

æ–‡æœ¬é©±åŠ¨ã€æ°¸ä¹…è§†å›¾ç”Ÿæˆã€3D ä¸€è‡´æ€§ã€ç½‘æ ¼è¡¨ç¤ºã€è§†é¢‘ç”Ÿæˆ





### 10ã€Scalable Adaptive Computation for Iterative Generation

Introducing ï¼ˆä»‹ç»ï¼‰: A neural net architecture.

ä¸€ç§ç¥žç»ç½‘ç»œæž¶æž„ã€‚



Paperï¼ˆè®ºæ–‡åœ°å€ï¼‰: 2022 [ Scalable Adaptive Computation for Iterative Generation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2212.11972)



Dateï¼ˆæ—¥æœŸï¼‰ï¼š2022å¹´12æœˆ23æ—¥

Summaryï¼ˆæ€»ç»“ï¼‰ï¼š

> The Recurrent Interface Network (RIN) is a neural net architecture that allocates computation adaptively to the input according to the distribution of information, allowing it to scale to iterative generation of high-dimensional data. RINs yield state-of-the-art image and video generation without cascades or guidance, while being domain-agnostic and up to 10x more efficient compared to specialized 2D and 3D U-Nets.
>
> å¾ªçŽ¯æŽ¥å£ç½‘ç»œï¼ˆRINï¼‰æ˜¯ä¸€ç§ç¥žç»ç½‘ç»œæž¶æž„ï¼Œå®ƒæ ¹æ®ä¿¡æ¯çš„åˆ†å¸ƒè‡ªé€‚åº”åœ°å°†è®¡ç®—åˆ†é…ç»™è¾“å…¥ï¼Œä»Žè€Œä½¿å…¶èƒ½å¤Ÿæ‰©å±•åˆ°é«˜ç»´æ•°æ®çš„è¿­ä»£ç”Ÿæˆã€‚ RIN æ— éœ€çº§è”æˆ–å¼•å¯¼å³å¯ç”Ÿæˆæœ€å…ˆè¿›çš„å›¾åƒå’Œè§†é¢‘ï¼ŒåŒæ—¶ä¸Žé¢†åŸŸæ— å…³ï¼Œå¹¶ä¸”ä¸Žä¸“é—¨çš„ 2D å’Œ 3D U-Net ç›¸æ¯”ï¼Œæ•ˆçŽ‡æé«˜äº† 10 å€ã€‚
>



Tagsï¼ˆæ ‡ç­¾ï¼‰ï¼š

neural networks, iterative generation, image generation, video generation

ç¥žç»ç½‘ç»œã€è¿­ä»£ç”Ÿæˆã€å›¾åƒç”Ÿæˆã€è§†é¢‘ç”Ÿæˆ

### 11ã€Keras documentation: Denoising Diffusion Probabilistic Model

Introducing ï¼ˆä»‹ç»ï¼‰: We implement the Denoising Diffusion Probabilistic Models paper or DDPMs for short in this code example.

æˆ‘ä»¬åœ¨æ­¤ä»£ç ç¤ºä¾‹ä¸­å®žçŽ°äº†åŽ»å™ªæ‰©æ•£æ¦‚çŽ‡æ¨¡åž‹è®ºæ–‡ï¼ˆç®€ç§° DDPMï¼‰ã€‚



Websiteï¼ˆå®˜æ–¹ç½‘ç«™ï¼‰: https://keras.io/examples/generative/ddpm/

> ##### Introduction ä»‹ç»
>
> Generative modeling experienced tremendous growth in the last five years. Models like VAEs, GANs, and flow-based models proved to be a great success in generating high-quality content, especially images. Diffusion models are a new type of generative model that has proven to be better than previous approaches.
> ç”Ÿæˆå»ºæ¨¡åœ¨è¿‡åŽ»äº”å¹´ä¸­ç»åŽ†äº†å·¨å¤§çš„å¢žé•¿ã€‚äº‹å®žè¯æ˜Žï¼ŒVAEã€GAN å’ŒåŸºäºŽæµçš„æ¨¡åž‹ç­‰æ¨¡åž‹åœ¨ç”Ÿæˆé«˜è´¨é‡å†…å®¹ï¼ˆå°¤å…¶æ˜¯å›¾åƒï¼‰æ–¹é¢å–å¾—äº†å·¨å¤§æˆåŠŸã€‚æ‰©æ•£æ¨¡åž‹æ˜¯ä¸€ç§æ–°åž‹çš„ç”Ÿæˆæ¨¡åž‹ï¼Œå·²è¢«è¯æ˜Žæ¯”ä»¥å‰çš„æ–¹æ³•æ›´å¥½ã€‚
>
> We implement the Denoising Diffusion Probabilistic Models paper or DDPMs for short in this code example. It was the first paper demonstrating the use of diffusion models for generating high-quality images. The authors proved that a certain parameterization of diffusion models reveals an equivalence with denoising score matching over multiple noise levels during training and with annealed Langevin dynamics during sampling that generates the best quality results.
> æˆ‘ä»¬åœ¨æ­¤ä»£ç ç¤ºä¾‹ä¸­å®žçŽ°äº†åŽ»å™ªæ‰©æ•£æ¦‚çŽ‡æ¨¡åž‹è®ºæ–‡ï¼ˆç®€ç§° DDPMï¼‰ã€‚è¿™æ˜¯ç¬¬ä¸€ç¯‡æ¼”ç¤ºå¦‚ä½•ä½¿ç”¨æ‰©æ•£æ¨¡åž‹ç”Ÿæˆé«˜è´¨é‡å›¾åƒçš„è®ºæ–‡ã€‚ä½œè€…è¯æ˜Žï¼Œæ‰©æ•£æ¨¡åž‹çš„æŸäº›å‚æ•°åŒ–æ­ç¤ºäº†è®­ç»ƒæœŸé—´å¤šä¸ªå™ªå£°çº§åˆ«çš„åŽ»å™ªåˆ†æ•°åŒ¹é…ä»¥åŠé‡‡æ ·æœŸé—´é€€ç«çš„æœ—ä¹‹ä¸‡åŠ¨åŠ›å­¦çš„ç­‰ä»·æ€§ï¼Œä»Žè€Œäº§ç”Ÿæœ€ä½³è´¨é‡çš„ç»“æžœã€‚
>
> ##### Conclusion ç»“è®º
>
> We successfully implemented and trained a diffusion model exactly in the same fashion as implemented by the authors of the DDPMs paper. You can find the original implementation here.
> æˆ‘ä»¬æˆåŠŸåœ°å®žçŽ°å¹¶è®­ç»ƒäº†ä¸€ä¸ªæ‰©æ•£æ¨¡åž‹ï¼Œå…¶æ–¹å¼ä¸Ž DDPM è®ºæ–‡ä½œè€…æ‰€é‡‡ç”¨çš„æ–¹å¼å®Œå…¨ç›¸åŒã€‚æ‚¨å¯ä»¥åœ¨è¿™é‡Œæ‰¾åˆ°åŽŸå§‹å®žçŽ°ã€‚

The original implementation ï¼ˆåŽŸå§‹å®žçŽ°ï¼‰ï¼šhttps://github.com/hojonathanho/diffusion

GitHubï¼ˆä»£ç åœ°å€ï¼‰ï¼šhttps://github.com/keras-team/keras-io/blob/master/examples/generative/ddpm.py

View in Colabï¼ˆåœ¨ Colab ä¸­æŸ¥çœ‹ï¼‰ï¼šhttps://colab.research.google.com/github/keras-team/keras-io/blob/master/examples/generative/ipynb/ddpm.ipynb

Dateï¼ˆæ—¥æœŸï¼‰ï¼š2022å¹´12æœˆ13æ—¥

Summaryï¼ˆæ€»ç»“ï¼‰ï¼š

> This URL link  above is to the Keras documentation for the Denoising Diffusion Probabilistic Model (DDPM), which is a generative model that can be used for image and video generation. The page provides an overview of the model and its architecture, as well as code examples for training and using the model.
>
> ä¸Šé¢çš„ URL é“¾æŽ¥æ˜¯åŽ»å™ªæ‰©æ•£æ¦‚çŽ‡æ¨¡åž‹ (DDPM) çš„ Keras æ–‡æ¡£ï¼ŒDDPM æ˜¯ä¸€ç§å¯ç”¨äºŽå›¾åƒå’Œè§†é¢‘ç”Ÿæˆçš„ç”Ÿæˆæ¨¡åž‹ã€‚è¯¥é¡µé¢æä¾›äº†æ¨¡åž‹åŠå…¶æž¶æž„çš„æ¦‚è¿°ï¼Œä»¥åŠç”¨äºŽè®­ç»ƒå’Œä½¿ç”¨æ¨¡åž‹çš„ä»£ç ç¤ºä¾‹ã€‚
>



Tagsï¼ˆæ ‡ç­¾ï¼‰ï¼š

### 25ã€Colossyan

Introducing ï¼ˆä»‹ç»ï¼‰:  Colossyan is among the first companies building tools to enable video production with the help of AI and [machine learning](https://www.unite.ai/what-is-machine-learning/) algorithms. Their tool can be used for everything from HR training videos to YouTube clips, and aims to make creating video content easier and more accessible to all.

This video generator enables you to choose from a diverse range of avatars and provide the avatar with a script. After your first video is generated you can then target different regions by auto-translating your whole video with the touch of a button. You can easily change accents and clothing. Choose from over 120 languages.

Here are some of the options:

Pick from our selection of commercially available synthetic AI presenters to connect with your audience.
Add Subtitles to your AI videos.
Personalize videos with different accents.
Enhance video messages through screen recordings.
Automated Translation.

### 26ã€NeverEndsï¼ˆ2.0ï¼‰

Introducing ï¼ˆä»‹ç»ï¼‰: AI video rookie NeverEnds is an AI tool that can generate videos from text and images. Recently, version 2.0 was launched, adding Tuxing video function and supporting mobile phone experience. - NeverEnds emphasizes AI videos that are more **realistic and practical** - **Strengthens the characterization of AI videos** - **Lowers the operating threshold** After a simple test, it performed very well on animation and advertising videos good. It is said that the next step will be to integrate text and voice functions, which can directly edit and produce videos, creating a low-cost, low-threshold AI video full-process video production tool.

### 27ã€LaVie

Introducing ï¼ˆä»‹ç»ï¼‰: The LaVie model is a large model that can generate videos based on text prompts. It is also a cascade model connected by three models. The paper on the LaVie model was made public at the end of September. However, the model pre-training results were open sourced in mid-to-early November. This model has a total of 3 billion parameters and is composed of three model cascades.

LaVie demonstrates extremely high quality in generating videos. This is mainly due to its three-part architecture: basic text-to-video (T2V) model, temporal interpolation model and video super-resolution model. This integrated approach allows LaVie to generate temporally coherent and smooth videos while maintaining high visual quality.

LaVieæ¨¡åž‹æ˜¯ä¸€ä¸ªå¯ä»¥åŸºäºŽæ–‡æœ¬æç¤ºç”Ÿæˆè§†é¢‘çš„å¤§æ¨¡åž‹ï¼Œä¹Ÿæ˜¯ä¸‰ä¸ªæ¨¡åž‹è¿žæŽ¥çš„çº§è”æ¨¡åž‹ã€‚**LaVieæ¨¡åž‹çš„è®ºæ–‡åœ¨9æœˆåº•å°±å·²ç»å…¬å¼€ã€‚ä½†æ˜¯æ¨¡åž‹é¢„è®­ç»ƒç»“æžœæ˜¯11æœˆä¸­ä¸Šæ—¬å¼€æºï¼Œè¿™ä¸ªæ¨¡åž‹å‚æ•°å…±30äº¿**ï¼Œç”±ä¸‰ä¸ªæ¨¡åž‹çº§è”ç»„æˆã€‚

LaVieåœ¨ç”Ÿæˆè§†é¢‘æ–¹é¢å±•çŽ°å‡ºäº†æžé«˜çš„è´¨é‡ã€‚è¿™ä¸»è¦å¾—ç›ŠäºŽå®ƒçš„ä¸‰éƒ¨åˆ†æž¶æž„ï¼šåŸºç¡€çš„æ–‡æœ¬åˆ°è§†é¢‘ï¼ˆT2Vï¼‰æ¨¡åž‹ã€æ—¶é—´æ’å€¼æ¨¡åž‹å’Œè§†é¢‘è¶…åˆ†è¾¨çŽ‡æ¨¡åž‹ã€‚è¿™ç§é›†æˆæ–¹æ³•å…è®¸LaVieåœ¨ä¿æŒé«˜è§†è§‰è´¨é‡çš„åŒæ—¶ï¼Œç”Ÿæˆåœ¨æ—¶é—´ä¸Šè¿žè´¯å’Œæµç•…çš„è§†é¢‘ã€‚



Paperï¼ˆè®ºæ–‡ï¼‰ï¼š2023 [LAVIE: High-Quality Video Generation with Cascaded Latent Diffusion Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2309.15103)

GitHubï¼ˆä»£ç åœ°å€ï¼‰ï¼šhttps://github.com/Vchitect/LaVie
